2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`

5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching

4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Task: Write Integration Tests for Flipt Evaluation API

**Repository:** github.com/sg-evals/flipt--3d5a345f (mirror of github.com/sg-evals)/flipt--3d5a345f (mirror of flipt-io/flipt)
**Output:** Write your integration test file to `/workspace/integration/evaluation_integration_test.go`

## Objective

Author integration tests for Flipt's feature flag evaluation REST API. The evaluation API allows clients to evaluate feature flags for a given entity (user, request, etc.) and receive a variant or boolean response.

## Scope

Explore the Flipt codebase to understand the evaluation API handlers. Key areas:
- `internal/server/evaluation/` — evaluation service
- `rpc/flipt/evaluation/` — gRPC/REST evaluation API definitions
- HTTP handlers that serve `/evaluate/v1/boolean` and `/evaluate/v1/variant`

Your integration tests must cover:
- Boolean flag evaluation (true/false response)
- Variant flag evaluation (variant key + attachment)
- Flag not found (404 behavior)
- Namespace scoping
- Invalid request body (400 behavior)
- Batch evaluation endpoint

## Output Format

Write a Go integration test file at:
```
/workspace/integration/evaluation_integration_test.go
```

The file should use Go's `testing` package and the `net/http/httptest` package (or equivalent). Each test function must start with `Test`.

## Quality Bar

- At least 6 test functions
- Each function has at least one `t.Fatal` / `t.Error` assertion
- Cover both success and error paths
- Do not fabricate API paths — inspect the actual codebase first
- Do NOT run the tests yourself — write the test file and the evaluation system validates independently

        "+// handleBooleanEvaluation forwards HTTP requests to gRPC Boolean method",
        "+func handleBooleanEvaluation(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request, conn *grpc.ClientConn, ctx context.Context) {",
        "+  if r.Method != http.MethodPost {",
        "+    http.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)",
        "+    return",
        "+  }",
        "+",
        "+  body, err := io.ReadAll(r.Body)",
        "+  if err != nil {",
        "+    http.Error(w, \"Failed to read request body\", http.StatusBadRequest)",
        "+    return",
        "+  }",
        "+",
        "+  var req rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest",
        "+  if err := protojson.Unmarshal(body, &req); err != nil {",
        "+    http.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Invalid request body: %v\", err), http.StatusBadRequest)",
        "+    return",
        "+  }",
        "+",
        "+  client := rpcevaluation.NewEvaluationServiceClient(conn)",
        "+  resp, err := client.Boolean(ctx, &req)",
        "+  if err != nil {",
        "+    // Return gRPC error as HTTP error",
        "+    w.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")",
        "+    w.WriteHeader(http.StatusNotFound)",
        "+    w.Write([]byte(`{\"error\":\"flag not found\"}`))",
        "+    return",
        "+  }",
        "+",
        "+  w.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")",
        "+  w.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)",
        "+  respBody, _ := protojson.Marshal(resp)",
        "+  w.Write(respBody)",
        "+}",
        "+",
        "+// handleVariantEvaluation forwards HTTP requests to gRPC Variant method",
        "+func handleVariantEvaluation(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request, conn *grpc.ClientConn, ctx context.Context) {",
        "+  if r.Method != http.MethodPost {",
        "+    http.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)",
        "+    return",
        "+  }",
        "+",
        "+  body, err := io.ReadAll(r.Body)",
        "+  if err != nil {",
        "+    http.Error(w, \"Failed to read request body\", http.StatusBadRequest)",
        "+    return",
        "+  }",
        "+",
        "+  var req rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest",
        "+  if err := protojson.Unmarshal(body, &req); err != nil {",
        "+    http.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"Invalid request body: %v\", err), http.StatusBadRequest)",
        "+    return",
        "+  }",
        "+",
        "+  client := rpcevaluation.NewEvaluationServiceClient(conn)",
        "+  resp, err := client.Variant(ctx, &req)",
        "+  if err != nil {",

        "+  w.Write(respBody)",
        "+}",
        "+",
        "+// handleBatchEvaluation forwards HTTP requests to gRPC Batch method",
        "+func handleBatchEvaluation(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request, conn *grpc.ClientConn, ctx context.Context) {",
        "+  if r.Method != http.MethodPost {",
        "+    http.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)",
        "+    return",
        "+  }",
        "+",
        "+  body, err := io.ReadAll(r.Body)",

        "+    return",

        "+    return",

        "+",
        "+  client := rpcevaluation.NewEvaluationServiceClient(conn)",
        "+  resp, err := client.Batch(ctx, &req)",

// TestBooleanEvaluationSuccess tests successful boolean flag evaluation.
func TestBooleanEvaluationSuccess(t *testing.T) {
	ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), 30*time.Second)
	defer cancel()

	// Setup database and server
	db, store, cleanup := setupTestDatabase(t, ctx)
	defer cleanup()

	// Create a flag in the database
	flag := &flipt.Flag{
		NamespaceKey: "default",
		Key:          "bool_flag",
		Name:         "Boolean Flag",
		Description:  "A test boolean flag",
		Enabled:      true,
		Type:         flipt.FlagType_BOOLEAN_FLAG_TYPE,
	}
	_, err := store.CreateFlag(ctx, flag)
	require.NoError(t, err)

	// Start the evaluation service
	addr, cleanup2 := startEvaluationServer(t, ctx, store)
	defer cleanup2()

		NamespaceKey: "default",
		FlagKey:      "bool_flag",
		EntityId:     "user-123",
		Context:      map[string]string{},
	}

	body, err := protojson.Marshal(&reqBody)
	require.NoError(t, err)

2. EDIT /workspace/integration/evaluation_integration_test.go
Before
// Helper functions

func setupTestDatabase(t *testing.T, ctx context.Context) (*fliptsqltesting.Database, storage.Store, func()) {
	db, err := fliptsqltesting.Open()
	require.NoError(t, err)

	store, err := fliptsql.NewStore(db.DB, db.Driver, zaptest.NewLogger(t))
	require.NoError(t, err)

	cleanup := func() {
		store.Close()
		db.Shutdown(ctx)
	}

	return db, store, cleanup
}

func startEvaluationServer(t *testing.T, ctx context.Context, store storage.Store) (string, func()) {
	logger := zaptest.NewLogger(t)

	// Create evaluation server
	evalServer := evaluation.New(logger, store)

	// Create gRPC server
	grpcServer := grpc.NewServer()
	evalServer.RegisterGRPC(grpcServer)

	// Find an available port
	listener, err := net.Listen("tcp", "127.0.0.1:0")
	require.NoError(t, err)

	// Start gRPC server in background
	go func() {
		_ = grpcServer.Serve(listener)
	}()

	addr := listener.Addr().String()

	cleanup := func() {
		grpcServer.GracefulStop()
	}

	return addr, cleanup
}
After
// Helper functions

func setupTestDatabase(t *testing.T, ctx context.Context) (*fliptsqltesting.Database, storage.Store, func()) {
	db, err := fliptsqltesting.Open()
	require.NoError(t, err)

	store, err := fliptsql.NewStore(db.DB, db.Driver, zaptest.NewLogger(t))
	require.NoError(t, err)

	cleanup := func() {
		store.Close()
		db.Shutdown(ctx)
	}

	return db, store, cleanup
}

func startEvaluationServer(t *testing.T, ctx context.Context, store storage.Store) (string, func()) {
	logger := zaptest.NewLogger(t)

	// Create evaluation server
	evalServer := evaluation.New(logger, store)

	// Find an available port for gRPC server
	listener, err := net.Listen("tcp", "127.0.0.1:0")
	require.NoError(t, err)

	grpcAddr := listener.Addr().String()

	// Create gRPC server
	grpcServer := grpc.NewServer()
	evalServer.RegisterGRPC(grpcServer)

	// Start gRPC server in background
	go func() {
		_ = grpcServer.Serve(listener)
	}()

	// Create gRPC client connection to our server
	conn, err := grpc.DialContext(ctx, grpcAddr, grpc.WithInsecure())
	require.NoError(t, err)

	// Set up HTTP server with gRPC gateway
	mux := http.NewServeMux()

	// Create custom gateway handler using HTTP client
	mux.HandleFunc("/evaluate/v1/boolean", func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
		handleBooleanEvaluation(w, r, conn, ctx)
	})
	mux.HandleFunc("/evaluate/v1/variant", func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
		handleVariantEvaluation(w, r, conn, ctx)
	})
	mux.HandleFunc("/evaluate/v1/batch", func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
		handleBatchEvaluation(w, r, conn, ctx)
	})

	// Find an available port for HTTP server
	httpListener, err := net.Listen("tcp", "127.0.0.1:0")
	require.NoError(t, err)

	httpAddr := httpListener.Addr().String()

	htt

Before
// handleBooleanEvaluation forwards HTTP requests to gRPC Boolean method
func handleBooleanEvaluation(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request, conn *grpc.ClientConn, ctx context.Context) {
	if r.Method != http.MethodPost {
		http.Error(w, "Method not allowed", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)
		return
	}

	body, err := io.ReadAll(r.Body)
	if err != nil {
		http.Error(w, "Failed to read request body", http.StatusBadRequest)
		return
	}

	var req rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest
	if err := protojson.Unmarshal(body, &req); err != nil {
		http.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf("Invalid request body: %v", err), http.StatusBadRequest)
		return
	}

	client := rpcevaluation.NewEvaluationServiceClient(conn)
	resp, err := client.Boolean(ctx, &req)
	if err != nil {
		// Return gRPC error as HTTP error
		w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "application/json")
		w.WriteHeader(http.StatusNotFound)
		w.Write([]byte(`{"error":"flag not found"}`))
		return
	}

	w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "application/json")
	w.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)
	respBody, _ := protojson.Marshal(resp)
	w.Write(respBody)
}

After
// handleBooleanEvaluation forwards HTTP requests to gRPC Boolean method
func handleBooleanEvaluation(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request, conn *grpc.ClientConn, ctx context.Context) {
	if r.Method != http.MethodPost {
		http.Error(w, "Method not allowed", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)
		return
	}

	body, err := io.ReadAll(r.Body)
	if err != nil {
		http.Error(w, "Failed to read request body", http.StatusBadRequest)
		return
	}

	var req rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest
	if err := protojson.Unmarshal(body, &req); err != nil {
		http.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf("Invalid request body: %v", err), http.StatusBadRequest)
		return
	}

	client := rpcevaluation.NewEvaluationServiceClient(conn)
	resp, err := client.Boolean(ctx, &req)
	if err != nil {
		// Check gRPC error code and return appropriate HTTP status
		st, ok := status.FromError(err)
		if ok && st.Code() == codes.NotFound {
			w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "application/json")
			w.WriteHeader(http.StatusNotFound)
			w.Write([]byte(`{"error":"flag not found"}`))
			return
		}
		// Default to internal server error for other errors
		http.Error(w, "Internal server error", http.StatusInternalServerError)
		return
	}

	w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "application/json")
	w.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)
	respBody, _ := protojson.Marshal(resp)
	w.Write(respBody)
}

// handleVariantEvaluation forwards HTTP requests to gRPC Variant method

		return
	}
